dark:text-white mb-1 not-first:mt-4"><span class="flex-1">Design patterns</span><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" group-hover:text-stone-500 text-stone-400 dark:text-stone-600" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></div></summary><ul><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/organization"><span class="">Organization/Team</span></a></li><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/history-patterns"><span class="">History Patterns</span></a></li></ul></details></div></li></ul></div></li></ul><div aria-hidden="true" class="h-12 right-0 sticky bottom-0 left-0 bg-linear-to-t from-white  to-transparent dark:from-stone-950 hidden md:block"></div></div></div></div><div class="md:col-span-8 lg:col-span-9 flex gap-12"><div class="w-full" data-pagefind-body="true" data-pagefind-meta="framework: react"><div class="overflow-hidden pb-8 pt-[calc(61px+2rem)] md:pt-8 md:max-w-3xl mx-auto prose dark:prose-invert dark:prose-code:bg-stone-900"><h1 id="colists">CoLists</h1>
<p>CoLists are ordered collections that work like JavaScript arrays. They provide indexed access, iteration methods, and length properties, making them perfect for managing sequences of items.</p>
<h2 id="creating-colists" class="group"><a href="#creating-colists" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Creating CoLists</span></h2>
<p>CoLists are defined by specifying the type of items they contain:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-visible wrap-break-word whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;_.line]:whitespace-pre-wrap border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> z } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfResources</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> ListOfResources</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfResources>;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfTasks>;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> ListOfTasksInitShape</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">input</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfTasks>; </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// type accepted by `ListOfTasks.create`</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>To create a <code>CoList</code>:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Create an empty list</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> resources</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">())</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([]);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Create a list with initial items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> tasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task)</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  { title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Prepare soil beds"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "in-progress"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  { title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Order compost"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "todo"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">]);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="ownership" class="group"><a href="#ownership" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Ownership</span></h3>
<p>Like other CoValues, you can specify ownership when creating CoLists.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Create with shared ownership</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> teamGroup</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Group</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">teamGroup</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.addMember</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(colleagueAccount</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "writer"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> teamList</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task)</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([]</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { owner</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> teamGroup });</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See <a href="/docs/react/permissions-and-sharing/overview">Groups as permission scopes</a> for more information on how to use groups to control access to CoLists.</p>
<h2 id="reading-from-colists" class="group"><a href="#reading-from-colists" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Reading from CoLists</span></h2>
<p>CoLists support standard array access patterns:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Access by index</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> firstTask</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> tasks[</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">0</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">];</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">firstTask</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.title); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// "Prepare soil beds"</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Get list length</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">tasks</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">length</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// 2</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Iteration</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">tasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.forEach</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((task) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.title);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">  // "Prepare soil beds"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">  // "Order compost"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Array methods</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> todoTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> tasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.filter</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((task) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.status </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "todo"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">todoTasks</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">length</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// 1</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="updating-colists" class="group"><a href="#updating-colists" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Updating CoLists</span></h2>
<p>Methods to update a CoList&#x27;s items are grouped inside the <code>$jazz</code> namespace:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Add items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"Tomatoes"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Add to end</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.unshift</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"Lettuce"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Add to beginning</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">tasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">  // Add complex items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Install irrigation"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // (Jazz will create</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "todo"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // the CoValue for you!)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Replace items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">0</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Cucumber"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Replace by index</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Modify nested items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">tasks[</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">0</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">].</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"status"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "complete"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Update properties of references</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="soft-deletion" class="group"><a href="#soft-deletion" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Soft Deletion</span></h3>
<p>You can do a soft deletion by using a deleted flag, then creating a helper method that explicitly filters out items where the deleted property is true.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark has-diff" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"todo"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "in-progress"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "complete"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  deleted</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">())</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Task;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfTasks;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> getCurrentTasks</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(list</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { $each</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> }>) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  return</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> list</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.filter</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((task)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> task </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">is</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">Task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">> </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> !</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.deleted);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">async</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> main</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> myTaskList</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([]);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  myTaskList</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Tomatoes"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "todo"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    deleted</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> false</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  myTaskList</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Cucumbers"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "todo"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    deleted</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  myTaskList</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Carrots"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "todo"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> activeTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> getCurrentTasks</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(myTaskList);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">activeTasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((task) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.title));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">  // Output: ["Tomatoes", "Carrots"]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>There are several benefits to soft deletions:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>recoverablity</strong> - Nothing is truly deleted, so recovery is possible in the future</li>
<li><strong>data integrity</strong> - Relationships can be maintained between current and deleted values</li>
<li><strong>auditable</strong> - The data can still be accessed, good for audit trails and checking compliance</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="deleting-items" class="group"><a href="#deleting-items" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Deleting Items</span></h3>
<p>Jazz provides two methods to retain or remove items from a CoList:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.remove</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">2</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// By index</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(resources); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ["Cucumber", "Peppers"]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.remove</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((item) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> item </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Cucumber"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Or by predicate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(resources); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ["Tomatoes", "Peppers"]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Keep only items matching the predicate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.retain</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((item) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> item </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!==</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Cucumber"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(resources); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ["Tomatoes", "Peppers"]</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>You can also remove specific items by index with <code>splice</code>, or remove the first or last item with <code>pop</code> or <code>shift</code>:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove 2 items starting at index 1</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.splice</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">1</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 2</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(resources); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ["Tomatoes"]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove a single item at index 0</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.splice</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">0</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 1</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(resources); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ["Cucumber", "Peppers"]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> lastItem</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.pop</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove and return last item</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.shift</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove first item</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="array-methods" class="group"><a href="#array-methods" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Array Methods</span></h3>
<p><code>CoList</code>s support the standard JavaScript array methods you already know. Methods that mutate the array
are grouped inside the <code>$jazz</code> namespace.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Add multiple items at once</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"Tomatoes"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Basil"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Peppers"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Find items</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> basil</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.find</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((r) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> r </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Basil"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Filter (returns regular array, not a CoList)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> tItems</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.filter</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((r) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> r</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.startsWith</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"T"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(tItems); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ["Tomatoes"]</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="type-safety" class="group"><a href="#type-safety" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Type Safety</span></h3>
<p>CoLists maintain type safety for their items:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del="3 4"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// TypeScript catches type errors</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"Carrots"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ✓ Valid string</span></span>
<span class="line diff remove"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">resources</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">42</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ✗ Type error: expected string</span></span>
<span class="line diff remove"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Argument of type 'number' is not assignable to parameter of type 'string'</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// For lists of references</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">tasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.forEach</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((task) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.title); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// TypeScript knows task has title</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="best-practices" class="group"><a href="#best-practices" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Best Practices</span></h2>
<h3 id="common-patterns" class="group"><a href="#common-patterns" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Common Patterns</span></h3>
<h4 id="list-rendering" class="group"><a href="#list-rendering" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">List Rendering</span></h4>
<p>CoLists work well with UI rendering libraries:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> z } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// React example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> TaskList</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({ tasks }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { tasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfTasks> }) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  return</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">ul</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      {tasks.map((task) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">        task.$isLoaded ? (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">          &#x3C;li key</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">{task.$jazz.id}</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">            {task.title} - {task.status}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">          &#x3C;/li></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">        ) : null</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      )}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    &#x3C;/</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">ul</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  );</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="managing-relations" class="group"><a href="#managing-relations" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Managing Relations</span></h4>
<p>CoLists can be used to create one-to-many relationships:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> z } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"todo"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "in-progress"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "complete"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  get</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">Optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Project> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    return</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Project);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  get</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> tasks</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">List</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Task> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    return</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfTasks;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Garden Project"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  tasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Plant seedlings"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "todo"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // Add a reference to the project</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Add a task to a garden project</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">tasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.push</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(task);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Access the project from the task</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.project); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// { name: "Garden Project", tasks: [task] }</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="set-like-collections" class="group"><a href="#set-like-collections" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Set-like Collections</span></h4>
<p>CoLists, like JavaScript arrays, allow you to insert the same item multiple times. In some cases, you might want to have a collection of unique items (similar to a set). To achieve this, you can use a CoRecord with entries keyed on a unique identifier (for example, the CoValue ID).</p>
<p>You can read <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/comaps#creating-set-like-collections">more about this pattern here</a>.</p><div class="flex flex-row justify-start flex-wrap items-center gap-2 py-2"><strong>Was this page helpful?</strong><div><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-white dark:bg-black
